1063<div class="rpl-markup__inner">

1064<p>

1065</p>

1066 <div data-embed-button="tide_media" data-entity-embed-display="view_mode:media.embedded" data-entity-type="media" data-entity-uuid="80ec4175-33de-3385-a172-1fd06322bfe7" data-langcode="en" class="embedded-entity embedded-entity--media embedded-entity--media--image">

1067<article class="media media--type-image media--view-mode-embedded">

1068<div class="field field--name-field-media-image field--type-image field--label-hidden field__item">

1069<img src="https://content.dhhs.vic.gov.au/sites/default/files/tennis_14985210_1050x600.jpg" width="1050" height="600" alt="tennis_14985210_1050x600">

1073 <p>

1074Tennis is a very popular sport in Australia and is played by people of all ages. Tennis can be played by two people (called â€˜playing singlesâ€™) or four people (â€˜doublesâ€™). Players use racquets to hit a ball over a net into the other side of the court.<br>

1075 <br>

1076

1077A game of tennis involves a variety of types of play, including serving the ball over the net, rallies (when the ball is hit back and forth between opponents), fast movements and strategic game play.<br>

1078 <br>

1079

1080Tennis can be played as a sport or as a recreational activity with friends and family. Either way, playing tennis is a good sport to maintain your health, fitness, strength and agility. It has been calculated that an hour-long game of singles tennis burns around 600 calories for men and 420 calories for women.<br>

1081 <br>

1082

1083In addition to the fitness and physical health benefits, tennis also provides numerous social and mental health benefits as well.</p>

1084 <h2 id="health-benefits-of-tennis">

1085Health benefits of tennis</h2>

1086 <p>

1087Tennis can be a great workout and lots of fun. Playing tennis has many health benefits including:</p>

1088 <ul>

1089<li>

1090increasing aerobic capacities</li>

1091 <li>

1092lowering resting heart rate and blood pressure</li>

1093 <li>

1094improving metabolic function</li>

1095 <li>

1096increasing bone density</li>

1097 <li>

1098lowering body fat</li>

1099 <li>

1100improving muscle tone, strength and flexibility</li>

1101 <li>

1102increasing reaction times</li>

1103</ul>

1104 <h2 id="other-benefits-of-tennis">

1105Other benefits of tennis</h2>

1106 <p>

1107As well as being a great physical workout, tennis is also:</p>

1108 <ul>

1109<li>

1110a non-impact sport</li>

1111 <li>

1112a great way to meet people and spend time with friends</li>

1113 <li>

1114suitable for all ages and skill levels. Whatever your level, you can find someone of a similar ability to play with</li>

1115 <li>

1116helpful to reduce stress</li>

1117 <li>

1118not dependent on youth or strength â€“ you can play for a lifetime or start the game at any age</li>

1119 <li>

1120played all over Australia and through many parts of the world</li>

1121</ul>

1122 <h2 id="starting-playing-tennis">

1123Starting playing tennis</h2>

1124 <p>

1125Tennis is very popular in Australia and is played in organised competitions as well as social games. In order to play tennis you need a racquet, a ball, a court with a net, and an opponent.<br>

1126 <br>

1127

1128Club courts and public courts are available for hire in most suburbs and towns. If you canâ€™t find someone to play against, many tennis clubs host organised social play, competitions and tournaments that will provide fellow tennis players for you to play with and against. Alternatively, if you donâ€™t have a tennis partner, you can always practise your skills by hitting a tennis ball against a wall.</p>

1129 <h2 id="avoiding-tennis-injuries">

1130Avoiding tennis injuries</h2>

1131 <ul>

1132<li>

1133Avoid playing with a pre-existing illness or injury. If in doubt, talk to a doctor.</li>

1134 <li>

1135Warm up your muscles and joints before hitting the court.</li>

1136 <li>

1137Maintain an adequate fitness level. Undertake conditioning and training exercises specific to the physical demands of tennis.</li>

1138 <li>

1139Occasionally, injuries caused through repetition of strokes can occur in tennis. Correct technique and playing the volume of tennis appropriate to your fitness levels can prevent injury. Make sure you have plenty of fluids on hand and drink regularly.</li>

1140 <li>

1141Play at a level according to your age and physical condition.</li>

1142 <li>

1143If the court conditions are wet, consider playing indoors or postponing your match, especially if the surface is slippery.</li>

1144</ul>

1188 <h2 id="things-to-remember">

1189Things to remember</h2>

1190 <ul>

1191<li>

1192Tennis is a good sport for maintaining health, fitness, strength and agility. It also has social and psychological benefits.</li>

1193 <li>

1194You can play with a club or with friends and family as a social activity.</li>

1195 <li>

1196Make sure you have plenty of fluids on hand and rehydrate regularly.</li>

1197 <li>

1198Donâ€™t overdo it. Mix up your physical activity with other low-impact sports.</li>

Information about a therapy, service, product or treatment does not in any way endorse or support such therapy, service, product or treatment and is not intended to replace advice from your doctor or other registered health professional. The information and materials contained on this website are not intended to constitute a comprehensive guide concerning all aspects of the therapy, product or treatment described on the website. All users are urged to always seek advice from a registered health care professional for diagnosis and answers to their medical questions and to ascertain whether the particular therapy, service, product or treatment described on the website is suitable in their circumstances. The State of Victoria and the Department of Health&nbsp;shall not bear any liability for reliance by any user on the materials contained on this website.</p>

by people of all ages. Tennis can be played by two people (called â€˜playing singlesâ€™) or four people (â€˜doublesâ€™). Players use racquets to hit a ball over a net into the other side of the court.\u003Cbr \u002F\u003E\n\u003Cbr \u002F\u003E\nA game of tennis involves a variety of types of play, including serving the ball over the net, rallies (when the ball is hit back and forth between opponents), fast movements and strategic game play.\u003Cbr \u002F\u003E\n\u003Cbr \u002F\u003E\nTennis can be played as a sport or as a recreational activity with friends and family. Either way, playing tennis is a good sport to maintain your health, fitness, strength and agility. It has been calculated that an hour-long game of singles tennis burns around 600 calories for men and 420 calories for women.\u003Cbr \u002F\u003E\n\u003Cbr \u002F\u003E\nIn addition to the fitness and physical health benefits, tennis also provides numerous social and mental health benefits as well.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\n\u003Ch2\u003EHealth benefits of tennis\u003C\u002Fh2\u003E\n\n\u003Cp\u003ETennis can be a great workout and lots of fun. Playing tennis has many health benefits including:\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\n\u003Cul\u003E\n\t\u003Cli\u003Eincreasing aerobic capacities\u003C\u002Fli\u003E\n\t\u003Cli\u003Elowering resting heart rate and blood pressure\u003C\u002Fli\u003E\n\t\u003Cli\u003Eimproving metabolic function\u003C\u002Fli\u003E\n\t\u003Cli\u003Eincreasing bone density\u003C\u002Fli\u003E\n\t\u003Cli\u003Elowering body fat\u003C\u002Fli\u003E\n\t\u003Cli\u003Eimproving muscle tone, strength and flexibility\u003C\u002Fli\u003E\n\t\u003Cli\u003Eincreasing reaction times\u003C\u002Fli\u003E\n\u003C\u002Ful\u003E\n\n\u003Ch2\u003EOther benefits of tennis\u003C\u002Fh2\u003E\n\n\u003Cp\u003EAs well as being a great physical workout, tennis is also:\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\n\u003Cul\u003E\n\t\u003Cli\u003Ea non-impact sport\u003C\u002Fli\u003E\n\t\u003Cli\u003Ea great way to meet people and spend time with friends\u003C\u002Fli\u003E\n\t\u003Cli\u003Esuitable for all ages and skill levels. Whatever your level, you can find someone of a similar ability to play with\u003C\u002Fli\u003E\n\t\u003Cli\u003Ehelpful to reduce stress\u003C\u002Fli\u003E\n\t\u003Cli\u003Enot dependent on youth or strength â€“ you can play for a lifetime or start the game at any age\u003C\u002Fli\u003E\n\t\u003Cli\u003Eplayed all over Australia and through many parts of the world\u003C\u002Fli\u003E\n\u003C\u002Ful\u003E\n\n\u003Ch2\u003EStarting playing tennis\u003C\u002Fh2\u003E\n\n\u003Cp\u003ETennis is very popular in Australia and is played in organised competitions as well as social games. In order to play tennis you need a racquet, a ball, a court with a net, and an opponent.\u003Cbr \u002F\u003E\n\u003Cbr \u002F\u003E\nClub courts and public courts are available for hire in most suburbs and towns. If you canâ€™t find someone to play against, many tennis clubs host organised social play, competitions and tournaments that will provide fellow tennis players for you to play with and against. Alternatively, if you donâ€™t have a tennis partner, you can always practise your skills by hitting a tennis ball against a wall.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\n\u003Ch2\u003EAvoiding tennis injuries\u003C\u002Fh2\u003E\n\n\u003Cul\u003E\n\t\u003Cli\u003EAvoid playing with a pre-existing illness or injury. If in doubt, talk to a doctor.\u003C\u002Fli\u003E\n\t\u003Cli\u003EWarm up your muscles and joints before hitting the court.\u003C\u002Fli\u003E\n\t\u003Cli\u003EMaintain an adequate fitness level. Undertake conditioning and training exercises specific to the physical demands of tennis.\u003C\u002Fli\u003E\n\t\u003Cli\u003EOccasionally, injuries caused through repetition of strokes can occur in tennis. Correct technique and playing the volume of tennis appropriate to your fitness levels can prevent injury. Make sure you have plenty of fluids on hand and drink regularly.\u003C\u002Fli\u003E\n\t\u003Cli\u003EPlay at a level according to your age and physical condition.\u003C\u002Fli\u003E\n\t\u003Cli\u003EIf the court conditions are wet, consider playing indoors or postponing your match, especially if the surface is slippery.\u003C\u002Fli\u003E\n\u003C\u002Ful\u003E\n\n\u003Ch2\u003EWhere to get help\u003C\u002Fh2\u003E\n\n\u003Cul\u003E\n\t\u003Cli\u003ELocal council\u003C\u002Fli\u003E\n\t\u003Cli\u003ELocal tennis club\u003C\u002Fli\u003E\n\t\u003Cli\u003ETennis Victoria Tel. \u003Ca href=\"tel:0384208420\"\u003E(03) 8420 8420\u003C\u002Fa\u003E\u003C\u002Fli\u003E\n\t\u003Cli\u003E\u003Ca href=\"https:\u002F\u002Fsmartplay.com.au\u002F\"\u003ESmartplay\u003C\u002Fa\u003E Tel. \u003Ca href=\"tel:0396748777\"\u003E(03) 9674 8777\u003C\u002Fa\u003E\u003C\u002Fli\u003E\n\u003C\u002Ful\u003E\n\n\u003Ch2\u003EThings to remember\u003C\u002Fh2\u003E\n\n\u003Cul\u003E\n\t\u003Cli\u003ETennis is a good sport for maintaining health, fitness, strength and agility.
